I’m using the experimental `async` flag.

     1	/** @import { BlockStatement, Pattern, Statement } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ComponentClientTransformState, ComponentContext } from '../types' */
     4	import { extract_identifiers, is_expression_async } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
     5	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
     6	import { create_derived } from '../utils.js';
     7	import { get_value } from './shared/declarations.js';
     8	import { build_expression, add_svelte_meta } from './shared/utils.js';
     9	
    10	/**
    11	 * @param {AST.AwaitBlock} node
    12	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    13	 */
    14	export function AwaitBlock(node, context) {
    15	        context.state.template.push_comment();
    16	
    17	        // Visit {#await <expression>} first to ensure that scopes are in the correct order
    18	        const expression = b.thunk(
    19	                build_expression(context, node.expression, node.metadata.expression),
    20	                node.metadata.expression.has_await
    21	        );
    22	
    23	        let then_block;
    24	        let catch_block;
    25	
    26	        if (node.then) {
    27	                const then_context = {
    28	                        ...context,
    29	                        state: { ...context.state, transform: { ...context.state.transform } }
    30	                };
    31	                const argument = node.value && create_derived_block_argument(node.value, then_context);
    32	
    33	                /** @type {Pattern[]} */
    34	                const args = [b.id('$$anchor')];
    35	                if (argument) args.push(argument.id);
    36	
    37	                const declarations = argument?.declarations ?? [];
    38	                const block = /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (then_context.visit(node.then, then_context.state));
    39	
    40	                then_block = b.arrow(args, b.block([...declarations, ...block.body]));
    41	        }
    42	
    43	        if (node.catch) {
    44	                const catch_context = { ...context, state: { ...context.state } };
    45	                const argument = node.error && create_derived_block_argument(node.error, catch_context);
    46	
    47	                /** @type {Pattern[]} */
    48	                const args = [b.id('$$anchor')];
    49	                if (argument) args.push(argument.id);
    50	
    51	                const declarations = argument?.declarations ?? [];
    52	                const block = /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (
    53	                        catch_context.visit(node.catch, catch_context.state)
    54	                );
    55	
    56	                catch_block = b.arrow(args, b.block([...declarations, ...block.body]));
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        context.state.init.push(
    60	                add_svelte_meta(
    61	                        b.call(
    62	                                '$.await',
    63	                                context.state.node,
    64	                                expression,
    65	                                node.pending
    66	                                        ? b.arrow([b.id('$$anchor')], /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (context.visit(node.pending)))
    67	                                        : b.null,
    68	                                then_block,
    69	                                catch_block
    70	                        ),
    71	                        node,
    72	                        'await'
    73	                )
    74	        );
    75	}
    76	
    77	/**
    78	 * @param {Pattern} node
    79	 * @param {import('zimmerframe').Context<AST.SvelteNode, ComponentClientTransformState>} context
    80	 * @returns {{ id: Pattern, declarations: null | Statement[] }}
    81	 */
    82	function create_derived_block_argument(node, context) {
    83	        if (node.type === 'Identifier') {
    84	                context.state.transform[node.name] = { read: get_value };
    85	                return { id: node, declarations: null };
    86	        }
    87	
    88	        const pattern = /** @type {Pattern} */ (context.visit(node));
    89	        const identifiers = extract_identifiers(node);
    90	
    91	        const id = b.id('$$source');
    92	        const value = b.id('$$value');
    93	
    94	        const block = b.block([
    95	                b.var(pattern, b.call('$.get', id)),
    96	                b.return(b.object(identifiers.map((identifier) => b.prop('init', identifier, identifier))))
    97	        ]);
    98	
    99	        const declarations = [b.var(value, create_derived(context.state, block))];
   100	
   101	        for (const id of identifiers) {
   102	                context.state.transform[id.name] = { read: get_value };
   103	
   104	                declarations.push(
   105	                        b.var(id, create_derived(context.state, b.member(b.call('$.get', value), id)))
   106	                );
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        return { id, declarations };
   110	}
   111

     1	/** @import { AssignmentPattern, BlockStatement, Expression, Identifier, Statement } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../types' */
     4	import { dev } from '../../../../state.js';
     5	import { extract_paths } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
     6	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
     7	import { get_value } from './shared/declarations.js';
     8	
     9	/**
    10	 * @param {AST.SnippetBlock} node
    11	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    12	 */
    13	export function SnippetBlock(node, context) {
    14	        // TODO hoist where possible
    15	        /** @type {(Identifier | AssignmentPattern)[]} */
    16	        const args = [b.id('$$anchor')];
    17	        const has_await = node.body.metadata.has_await || false;
    18	
    19	        /** @type {BlockStatement} */
    20	        let body;
    21	
    22	        /** @type {Statement[]} */
    23	        const declarations = [];
    24	
    25	        const transform = { ...context.state.transform };
    26	        const child_state = { ...context.state, transform };
    27	
    28	        for (let i = 0; i < node.parameters.length; i++) {
    29	                const argument = node.parameters[i];
    30	
    31	                if (!argument) continue;
    32	
    33	                if (argument.type === 'Identifier') {
    34	                        args.push(b.assignment_pattern(argument, b.id('$.noop')));
    35	                        transform[argument.name] = { read: b.call };
    36	
    37	                        continue;
    38	                }
    39	
    40	                let arg_alias = `$$arg${i}`;
    41	                args.push(b.id(arg_alias));
    42	
    43	                const { inserts, paths } = extract_paths(argument, b.maybe_call(b.id(arg_alias)));
    44	
    45	                for (const { id, value } of inserts) {
    46	                        id.name = context.state.scope.generate('$$array');
    47	                        transform[id.name] = { read: get_value };
    48	
    49	                        declarations.push(
    50	                                b.var(id, b.call('$.derived', /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(b.thunk(value)))))
    51	                        );
    52	                }
    53	
    54	                for (const path of paths) {
    55	                        const name = /** @type {Identifier} */ (path.node).name;
    56	                        const needs_derived = path.has_default_value; // to ensure that default value is only called once
    57	                        const fn = b.thunk(/** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(path.expression, child_state)));
    58	
    59	                        declarations.push(b.let(path.node, needs_derived ? b.call('$.derived_safe_equal', fn) : fn));
    60	
    61	                        transform[name] = {
    62	                                read: needs_derived ? get_value : b.call
    63	                        };
    64	
    65	                        // we need to eagerly evaluate the expression in order to hit any
    66	                        // 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
    67	                        if (dev) {
    68	                                declarations.push(b.stmt(transform[name].read(b.id(name))));
    69	                        }
    70	                }
    71	        }
    72	        const block = /** @type {BlockStatement} */ (context.visit(node.body, child_state)).body;
    73	        body = b.block([
    74	                dev ? b.stmt(b.call('$.validate_snippet_args', b.spread(b.id('arguments')))) : b.empty,
    75	                ...declarations,
    76	                ...block
    77	        ]);
    78	
    79	        // in dev we use a FunctionExpression (not arrow function) so we can use `arguments`
    80	        let snippet = dev
    81	                ? b.call(
    82	                                '$.wrap_snippet',
    83	                                b.id(context.state.analysis.name),
    84	                                b.function(null, args, body, has_await)
    85	                        )
    86	                : b.arrow(args, body, has_await);
    87	
    88	        const declaration = b.const(node.expression, snippet);
    89	
    90	        // Top-level snippets are hoisted so they can be referenced in the `<script>`
    91	        if (context.path.length === 1 && context.path[0].type === 'Fragment') {
    92	                if (node.metadata.can_hoist) {
    93	                        context.state.module_level_snippets.push(declaration);
    94	                } else {
    95	                        context.state.instance_level_snippets.push(declaration);
    96	                }
    97	        } else {
    98	                context.state.init.push(declaration);
    99	        }
   100	}
   101

    83	/**
    84	 * @type {Visitors}
    85	 */
    86	const visitors = {
    87	        _(node, { state, next, path }) {
    88	                const parent = path.at(-1);
    89	
    90	                /** @type {string[]} */
    91	                const ignores = [];
    92	
    93	                if (parent?.type === 'Fragment' && node.type !== 'Comment' && node.type !== 'Text') {
    94	                        const idx = parent.nodes.indexOf(/** @type {any} */ (node));
    95	
    96	                        for (let i = idx - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    97	                                const prev = parent.nodes[i];
    98	
    99	                                if (prev.type === 'Comment') {
   100	                                        ignores.push(
   101	                                                ...extract_svelte_ignore(
   102	                                                        prev.start + 4 /* '<!--'.length */,
   103	                                                        prev.data,
   104	                                                        state.analysis.runes
   105	                                                )
   106	                                        );
   107	                                } else if (prev.type !== 'Text') {
   108	                                        break;
   109	                                }
   110	                        }
   111	                } else {
   112	                        const comments = /** @type {any} */ (node).leadingComments;
   113	
   114	                        if (comments) {
   115	                                for (const comment of comments) {
   116	                                        ignores.push(
   117	                                                ...extract_svelte_ignore(
   118	                                                        comment.start + 2 /* '//'.length */,
   119	                                                        comment.value,
   120	                                                        state.analysis.runes
   121	                                                )
   122	                                        );
   123	                                }
   124	                        }
   125	                }
   126	
   127	                if (ignores.length > 0) {
   128	                        push_ignore(ignores);
   129	                }
   130	
   131	                ignore_map.set(node, structuredClone(ignore_stack));
   132	
   133	                const scope = state.scopes.get(node);
   134	                next(scope !== undefined && scope !== state.scope ? { ...state, scope } : state);
   135	
   136	                if (ignores.length > 0) {
   137	                        pop_ignore();
   138	                }
   139	        },

   201	/**
   202	 * @param {AST.Script | null} script
   203	 * @param {ScopeRoot} root
   204	 * @param {boolean} allow_reactive_declarations
   205	 * @param {Scope | null} parent
   206	 * @returns {Js}
   207	 */
   208	function js(script, root, allow_reactive_declarations, parent) {
   209	        /** @type {Program} */
   210	        const ast = script?.content ?? {
   211	                type: 'Program',
   212	                sourceType: 'module',
   213	                start: -1,
   214	                end: -1,
   215	                body: []
   216	        };
   217	
   218	        const { scope, scopes, has_await } = create_scopes(
   219	                ast,
   220	                root,
   221	                allow_reactive_declarations,
   222	                parent
   223	        );
   224	
   225	        return { ast, scope, scopes, has_await };
   226	}
   227	
   228	/**
   229	 * @param {string} filename
   230	 */
   231	function get_component_name(filename) {
   232	        const parts = filename.split(/[/\\]/);
   233	        const basename = /** @type {string} */ (parts.pop());
   234	        const last_dir = /** @type {string} */ (parts.at(-1));
   235	        let name = basename.replace('.svelte', '');
   236	        if (name === 'index' && last_dir && last_dir !== 'src') {
   237	                name = last_dir;
   238	        }
   239	        return name[0].toUpperCase() + name.slice(1);
   240	}
   241	
   242	const RESERVED = ['$$props', '$$restProps', '$$slots'];
   243	
   244	/**
   245	 * @param {string} source
   246	 * @param {ValidatedModuleCompileOptions} options
   247	 * @returns {Analysis}
   248	 */
   249	export function analyze_module(source, options) {
   250	        /** @type {AST.JSComment[]} */
   251	        const comments = [];
   252	
   253	        state.set_source(source);
   254	        const ast = parse(source, comments, false, false);
   255	
   256	        const { scope, scopes, has_await } = create_scopes(ast, new ScopeRoot(), false, null);
   257	
   258	        for (const [name, references] of scope.references) {
   259	                if (name[0] !== '$' || RESERVED.includes(name)) continue;
   260	                if (name === '$' || name[1] === '$') {
   261	                        e.global_reference_invalid(references[0].node, name);
   262	                }
   263	
   264	                const binding = scope.get(name.slice(1));
   265	
   266	                if (binding !== null && !is_rune(name)) {
   267	                        e.store_invalid_subscription_module(references[0].node);
   268	                }
   269	        }
   270	
   271	        /** @type {Analysis} */
   272	        const analysis = {
   273	                module: { ast, scope, scopes, has_await },
   274	                name: options.filename,
   275	                accessors: false,
   276	                runes: true,
   277	                immutable: true,
   278	                tracing: false,
   279	                async_deriveds: new Set(),
   280	                comments,
   281	                classes: new Map()
   282	        };
   283	
   284	        state.adjust({
   285	                dev: options.dev,
   286	                rootDir: options.rootDir,
   287	                runes: true
   288	        });
   289	
   290	        walk(
   291	                /** @type {Node} */ (ast),
   292	                {
   293	                        scope,
   294	                        scopes,
   295	                        analysis: /** @type {ComponentAnalysis} */ (analysis),
   296	                        state_fields: new Map(),
   297	                        // TODO the following are not needed for modules, but we have to pass them in order to avoid type error,
   298	                        // and reducing the type would result in a lot of tedious type casts elsewhere - find a good solution one day
   299	                        ast_type: /** @type {any} */ (null),
   300	                        component_slots: /** @type {Set<string>} */ (new Set()),
   301	                        expression: null,
   302	                        function_depth: 0,
   303	                        has_props_rune: false,
   304	                        options: /** @type {ValidatedCompileOptions} */ (options),
   305	                        fragment: null,
   306	                        parent_element: null,
   307	                        reactive_statement: null
   308	                },
   309	                visitors
   310	        );
   311	
   312	        return analysis;
   313	}

   315	/**
   316	 * @param {AST.Root} root
   317	 * @param {string} source
   318	 * @param {ValidatedCompileOptions} options
   319	 * @returns {ComponentAnalysis}
   320	 */
   321	export function analyze_component(root, source, options) {
   322	        const scope_root = new ScopeRoot();
   323	
   324	        const module = js(root.module, scope_root, false, null);
   325	        const instance = js(root.instance, scope_root, true, module.scope);
   326	
   327	        const { scope, scopes, has_await } = create_scopes(
   328	                root.fragment,
   329	                scope_root,
   330	                false,
   331	                instance.scope
   332	        );
   333	
   334	        /** @type {Template} */
   335	        const template = { ast: root.fragment, scope, scopes };
   336	
   337	        let synthetic_stores_legacy_check = [];
   338	
   339	        // create synthetic bindings for store subscriptions
   340	        for (const [name, references] of module.scope.references) {
   341	                if (name[0] !== '$' || RESERVED.includes(name)) continue;
   342	                if (name === '$' || name[1] === '$') {
   343	                        e.global_reference_invalid(references[0].node, name);
   344	                }
   345	
   346	                const store_name = name.slice(1);
   347	                const declaration = instance.scope.get(store_name);
   348	                const init = /** @type {Node | undefined} */ (declaration?.initial);
   349	
   350	                // If we're not in legacy mode through the compiler option, assume the user
   351	                // is referencing a rune and not a global store.
   352	                if (
   353	                        options.runes === false ||
   354	                        !is_rune(name) ||
   355	                        (declaration !== null &&
   356	                                // const state = $state(0) is valid
   357	                                (get_rune(init, instance.scope) === null ||
   358	                                        // rune-line names received as props are valid too (but we have to protect against $props as store)
   359	                                        (store_name !== 'props' && get_rune(init, instance.scope) === '$props')) &&
   360	                                // allow `import { derived } from 'svelte/store'` in the same file as `const x = $derived(..)` because one is not a subscription to the other
   361	                                !(
   362	                                        name === '$derived' &&
   363	                                        declaration.initial?.type === 'ImportDeclaration' &&
   364	                                        declaration.initial.source.value === 'svelte/store'
   365	                                ))
   366	                ) {
   367	                        let is_nested_store_subscription_node = undefined;
   368	                        search: for (const reference of references) {
   369	                                for (let i = reference.path.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   370	                                        const scope =
   371	                                                scopes.get(reference.path[i]) ||
   372	                                                module.scopes.get(reference.path[i]) ||
   373	                                                instance.scopes.get(reference.path[i]);
   374	                                        if (scope) {
   375	                                                const owner = scope?.owner(store_name);
   376	                                                if (!!owner && owner !== module.scope && owner !== instance.scope) {
   377	                                                        is_nested_store_subscription_node = reference.node;
   378	                                                        break search;
   379	                                                }
   380	                                                break;
   381	                                        }
   382	                                }
   383	                        }
   384	
   385	                        if (is_nested_store_subscription_node) {
   386	                                e.store_invalid_scoped_subscription(is_nested_store_subscription_node);
   387	                        }
   388	
   389	                        if (options.runes !== false) {
   390	                                if (declaration === null && /[a-z]/.test(store_name[0])) {
   391	                                        e.global_reference_invalid(references[0].node, name);
   392	                                } else if (declaration !== null && is_rune(name)) {
   393	                                        for (const { node, path } of references) {
   394	                                                if (path.at(-1)?.type === 'CallExpression') {
   395	                                                        w.store_rune_conflict(node, store_name);
   396	                                                }
   397	                                        }
   398	                                }
   399	                        }
   400	
   401	                        if (module.ast) {
   402	                                for (const { node, path } of references) {
   403	                                        // if the reference is inside module, error. this is a bit hacky but it works
   404	                                        if (
   405	                                                /** @type {number} */ (node.start) > /** @type {number} */ (module.ast.start) &&
   406	                                                /** @type {number} */ (node.end) < /** @type {number} */ (module.ast.end) &&
   407	                                                // const state = $state(0) is valid
   408	                                                get_rune(/** @type {Node} */ (path.at(-1)), module.scope) === null
   409	                                        ) {
   410	                                                e.store_invalid_subscription(node);
   411	                                        }
   412	                                }
   413	                        }
   414	
   415	                        // we push to the array because at this moment in time we can't be sure if we are in legacy
   416	                        // mode yet because we are still changing the module scope
   417	                        synthetic_stores_legacy_check.push(() => {
   418	                                // if we are creating a synthetic binding for a let declaration we should also declare
   419	                                // the declaration as state in case it's reassigned and we are not in runes mode (the function will
   420	                                // not be called if we are not in runes mode, that's why there's no !runes check here)
   421	                                if (
   422	                                        declaration !== null &&
   423	                                        declaration.kind === 'normal' &&
   424	                                        declaration.declaration_kind === 'let' &&
   425	                                        declaration.reassigned
   426	                                ) {
   427	                                        declaration.kind = 'state';
   428	                                }
   429	                        });
   430	
   431	                        const binding = instance.scope.declare(b.id(name), 'store_sub', 'synthetic');
   432	                        binding.references = references;
   433	                        instance.scope.references.set(name, references);
   434	                        module.scope.references.delete(name);
   435	                }
   436	        }
   437	
   438	        const component_name = get_component_name(options.filename);
   439	
   440	        const runes =
   441	                options.runes ??
   442	                (has_await || instance.has_await || Array.from(module.scope.references.keys()).some(is_rune));
   443	
   444	        if (!runes) {
   445	                for (let check of synthetic_stores_legacy_check) {
   446	                        check();
   447	                }
   448	        }
   449	
   450	        if (runes && root.module) {
   451	                const context = root.module.attributes.find((attribute) => attribute.name === 'context');
   452	                if (context) {
   453	                        w.script_context_deprecated(context);
   454	                }
   455	        }
   456	
   457	        const is_custom_element = !!options.customElementOptions || options.customElement;
   458	
   459	        // TODO remove all the ?? stuff, we don't need it now that we're validating the config
   460	        /** @type {ComponentAnalysis} */
   461	        const analysis = {
   462	                name: module.scope.generate(options.name ?? component_name),
   463	                root: scope_root,
   464	                module,
   465	                instance,
   466	                template,
   467	                comments: root.comments,
   468	                elements: [],
   469	                runes,
   470	                // if we are not in runes mode but we have no reserved references ($$props, $$restProps)
   471	                // and no `export let` we might be in a wannabe runes component that is using runes in an external
   472	                // module...we need to fallback to the runic behavior
   473	                maybe_runes:
   474	                        !runes &&
   475	                        // if they explicitly disabled runes, use the legacy behavior
   476	                        options.runes !== false &&
   477	                        ![...module.scope.references.keys()].some((name) =>
   478	                                ['$$props', '$$restProps'].includes(name)
   479	                        ) &&
   480	                        !instance.ast.body.some(
   481	                                (node) =>

   483	                                        (node.type === 'ExportNamedDeclaration' &&
   484	                                                ((node.declaration &&
   485	                                                        node.declaration.type === 'VariableDeclaration' &&
   486	                                                        node.declaration.kind === 'let') ||
   487	                                                        node.specifiers.some(

    70	        'Number.parseInt': [NUMBER, Number.parseInt],
    71	        String: [STRING, String],
    72	        'String.fromCharCode': [STRING, String.fromCharCode],
    73	        'String.fromCodePoint': [STRING, String.fromCodePoint]
    74	};
    75	
    76	/** @type {Record<string, any>} */
    77	const global_constants = {
    78	        'Math.PI': Math.PI,
    79	        'Math.E': Math.E,
    80	        'Math.LN10': Math.LN10,
    81	        'Math.LN2': Math.LN2,
    82	        'Math.LOG10E': Math.LOG10E,
    83	        'Math.LOG2E': Math.LOG2E,
    84	        'Math.SQRT2': Math.SQRT2,
    85	        'Math.SQRT1_2': Math.SQRT1_2
    86	};
    87	
    88	export class Binding {
    89	        /** @type {Scope} */
    90	        scope;
    91	
    92	        /** @type {Identifier} */
    93	        node;
    94	
    95	        /** @type {BindingKind} */
    96	        kind;
    97	
    98	        /** @type {DeclarationKind} */
    99	        declaration_kind;
   100	
   101	        /**
   102	         * What the value was initialized with.
   103	         * For destructured props such as `let { foo = 'bar' } = $props()` this is `'bar'` and not `$props()`
   104	         * @type {null | Expression | FunctionDeclaration | ClassDeclaration | ImportDeclaration | AST.EachBlock | AST.SnippetBlock}
   105	         */
   106	        initial = null;
   107	
   108	        /** @type {Array<{ node: Identifier; path: AST.SvelteNode[] }>} */
   109	        references = [];
   110	
   111	        /**
   112	         * For `legacy_reactive`: its reactive dependencies
   113	         * @type {Binding[]}
   114	         */
   115	        legacy_dependencies = [];
   116	
   117	        /**
   118	         * Legacy props: the `class` in `{ export klass as class}`. $props(): The `class` in { class: klass } = $props()
   119	         * @type {string | null}
   120	         */
   121	        prop_alias = null;
   122	
   123	        /**
   124	         * Additional metadata, varies per binding type
   125	         * @type {null | { inside_rest?: boolean; is_template_declaration?: boolean }}
   126	         */
   127	        metadata = null;
   128	
   129	        mutated = false;
   130	        reassigned = false;
   131	
   132	        /**
   133	         *
   134	         * @param {Scope} scope
   135	         * @param {Identifier} node
   136	         * @param {BindingKind} kind
   137	         * @param {DeclarationKind} declaration_kind
   138	         * @param {Binding['initial']} initial
   139	         */
   140	        constructor(scope, node, kind, declaration_kind, initial) {
   141	                this.scope = scope;
   142	                this.node = node;
   143	                this.initial = initial;
   144	                this.kind = kind;
   145	                this.declaration_kind = declaration_kind;
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        get updated() {
   149	                return this.mutated || this.reassigned;
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        /**
   153	         * @returns {this is Binding & { initial: ArrowFunctionExpression | FunctionDeclaration | FunctionExpression }}
   154	         */
   155	        is_function() {
   156	                if (this.updated) {
   157	                        // even if it's reassigned to another function,
   158	                        // we can't use it directly as e.g. an event handler
   159	                        return false;
   160	                }
   161	
   162	                const type = this.initial?.type;
   163	
   164	                return (
   165	                        type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' ||
   166	                        type === 'FunctionExpression' ||
   167	                        type === 'FunctionDeclaration'
   168	                );
   169	        }
   170	}
   171	
   172	class Evaluation {
   173	        /** @type {Set<any>} */
   174	        values;
   175	
   176	        /**
   177	         * True if there is exactly one possible value
   178	         * @readonly
   179	         * @type {boolean}
   180	         */
   181	        is_known = true;
   182	
   183	        /**
   184	         * True if the possible values contains `UNKNOWN`
   185	         * @readonly
   186	         * @type {boolean}
   187	         */
   188	        has_unknown = false;
   189	
   190	        /**
   191	         * True if the value is known to not be null/undefined
   192	         * @readonly
   193	         * @type {boolean}
   194	         */
   195	        is_defined = true;
   196	
   197	        /**
   198	         * True if the value is known to be a string
   199	         * @readonly
   200	         * @type {boolean}
   201	         */
   202	        is_string = true;
   203	
   204	        /**
   205	         * True if the value is known to be a number
   206	         * @readonly
   207	         * @type {boolean}
   208	         */
   209	        is_number = true;
   210	
   211	        /**
   212	         * True if the value is known to be a function
   213	         * @readonly
   214	         * @type {boolean}
   215	         */
   216	        is_function = true;
   217	
   218	        /**
   219	         * @readonly
   220	         * @type {any}
   221	         */
   222	        value = undefined;
   223	
   224	        /**
   225	         *
   226	         * @param {Scope} scope
   227	         * @param {Expression | FunctionDeclaration} expression
   228	         * @param {Set<any>} values
   229	         */
   230	        constructor(scope, expression, values) {
   231	                current_evaluations.set(expression, this);
   232	
   233	                this.values = values;
   234	
   235	                switch (expression.type) {
   236	                        case 'Literal': {
   237	                                this.values.add(expression.value);
   238	                                break;
   239	                        }
   240	
   241	                        case 'Identifier': {
   242	                                const binding = scope.get(expression.name);
   243	
   244	                                if (binding) {
   245	                                        if (
   246	                                                binding.initial?.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   247	                                                get_rune(binding.initial, scope) === '$props.id'
   248	                                        ) {
   249	                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   250	                                                break;
   251	                                        }
   252	
   253	                                        const is_prop =
   254	                                                binding.kind === 'prop' ||
   255	                                                binding.kind === 'rest_prop' ||
   256	                                                binding.kind === 'bindable_prop';
   257	
   258	                                        if (binding.initial?.type === 'EachBlock' && binding.initial.index === expression.name) {
   259	                                                this.values.add(NUMBER);
   260	                                                break;
   261	                                        }
   262	
   263	                                        if (!binding.updated && binding.initial !== null && !is_prop) {
   264	                                                binding.scope.evaluate(/** @type {Expression} */ (binding.initial), this.values);
   265	                                                break;
   266	                                        }
   267	                                } else if (expression.name === 'undefined') {
   268	                                        this.values.add(undefined);
   269	                                        break;
   270	                                }
   271	
   272	                                // TODO glean what we can from reassignments
   273	                                // TODO one day, expose props and imports somehow
   274	
   275	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   276	                                break;
   277	                        }
   278	
   279	                        case 'BinaryExpression': {
   280	                                const a = scope.evaluate(/** @type {Expression} */ (expression.left)); // `left` cannot be `PrivateIdentifier` unless operator is `in`
   281	                                const b = scope.evaluate(expression.right);
   282	
   283	                                if (a.is_known && b.is_known) {
   284	                                        this.values.add(binary[expression.operator](a.value, b.value));
   285	                                        break;
   286	                                }
   287	
   288	                                switch (expression.operator) {
   289	                                        case '!=':
   290	                                        case '!==':
   291	                                        case '<':
   292	                                        case '<=':
   293	                                        case '>':
   294	                                        case '>=':
   295	                                        case '==':
   296	                                        case '===':
   297	                                        case 'in':
   298	                                        case 'instanceof':
   299	                                                this.values.add(true);
   300	                                                this.values.add(false);
   301	                                                break;
   302	
   303	                                        case '%':
   304	                                        case '&':
   305	                                        case '*':
   306	                                        case '**':
   307	                                        case '-':
   308	                                        case '/':
   309	                                        case '<<':
   310	                                        case '>>':
   311	                                        case '>>>':
   312	                                        case '^':
   313	                                        case '|':
   314	                                                this.values.add(NUMBER);
   315	                                                break;
   316	
   317	                                        case '+':
   318	                                                if (a.is_string || b.is_string) {
   319	                                                        this.values.add(STRING);
   320	                                                } else if (a.is_number && b.is_number) {
   321	                                                        this.values.add(NUMBER);
   322	                                                } else {
   323	                                                        this.values.add(STRING);
   324	                                                        this.values.add(NUMBER);
   325	                                                }
   326	                                                break;
   327	
   328	                                        default:
   329	                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   330	                                }
   331	                                break;
   332	                        }
   333	
   334	                        case 'ConditionalExpression': {
   335	                                const test = scope.evaluate(expression.test);
   336	                                const consequent = scope.evaluate(expression.consequent);
   337	                                const alternate = scope.evaluate(expression.alternate);
   338	
   339	                                if (test.is_known) {
   340	                                        for (const value of (test.value ? consequent : alternate).values) {
   341	                                                this.values.add(value);
   342	                                        }
   343	                                } else {
   344	                                        for (const value of consequent.values) {
   345	                                                this.values.add(value);
   346	                                        }
   347	
   348	                                        for (const value of alternate.values) {
   349	                                                this.values.add(value);
   350	                                        }
   351	                                }
   352	                                break;
   353	                        }
   354	
   355	                        case 'LogicalExpression': {
   356	                                const a = scope.evaluate(expression.left);
   357	                                const b = scope.evaluate(expression.right);
   358	
   359	                                if (a.is_known) {
   360	                                        if (b.is_known) {
   361	                                                this.values.add(logical[expression.operator](a.value, b.value));
   362	                                                break;
   363	                                        }
   364	
   365	                                        if (
   366	                                                (expression.operator === '&&' && !a.value) ||
   367	                                                (expression.operator === '||' && a.value) ||
   368	                                                (expression.operator === '??' && a.value != null)
   369	                                        ) {
   370	                                                this.values.add(a.value);
   371	                                        } else {
   372	                                                for (const value of b.values) {
   373	                                                        this.values.add(value);
   374	                                                }
   375	                                        }
   376	
   377	                                        break;
   378	                                }
   379	
   380	                                for (const value of a.values) {
   381	                                        this.values.add(value);
   382	                                }
   383	
   384	                                for (const value of b.values) {
   385	                                        this.values.add(value);
   386	                                }
   387	                                break;
   388	                        }
   389	
   390	                        case 'UnaryExpression': {
   391	                                const argument = scope.evaluate(expression.argument);
   392	
   393	                                if (argument.is_known) {
   394	                                        this.values.add(unary[expression.operator](argument.value));
   395	                                        break;
   396	                                }
   397	
   398	                                switch (expression.operator) {
   399	                                        case '!':
   400	                                        case 'delete':
   401	                                                this.values.add(false);
   402	                                                this.values.add(true);
   403	                                                break;
   404	
   405	                                        case '+':
   406	                                        case '-':
   407	                                        case '~':
   408	                                                this.values.add(NUMBER);
   409	                                                break;
   410	
   411	                                        case 'typeof':
   412	                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   413	                                                break;
   414	
   415	                                        case 'void':
   416	                                                this.values.add(undefined);
   417	                                                break;
   418	
   419	                                        default:
   420	                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   421	                                }
   422	                                break;
   423	                        }
   424	
   425	                        case 'CallExpression': {
   426	                                const keypath = get_global_keypath(expression.callee, scope);
   427	
   428	                                if (keypath) {
   429	                                        if (is_rune(keypath)) {
   430	                                                const arg = /** @type {Expression | undefined} */ (expression.arguments[0]);
   431	
   432	                                                switch (keypath) {
   433	                                                        case '$state':
   434	                                                        case '$state.raw':
   435	                                                        case '$derived':
   436	                                                                if (arg) {
   437	                                                                        scope.evaluate(arg, this.values);
   438	                                                                } else {
   439	                                                                        this.values.add(undefined);
   440	                                                                }
   441	                                                                break;
   442	
   443	                                                        case '$props.id':
   444	                                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   445	                                                                break;
   446	
   447	                                                        case '$effect.tracking':
   448	                                                                this.values.add(false);
   449	                                                                this.values.add(true);
   450	                                                                break;
   451	
   452	                                                        case '$derived.by':
   453	                                                                if (arg?.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' && arg.body.type !== 'BlockStatement') {
   454	                                                                        scope.evaluate(arg.body, this.values);
   455	                                                                        break;
   456	                                                                }
   457	
   458	                                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   459	                                                                break;
   460	
   461	                                                        default: {
   462	                                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   463	                                                        }
   464	                                                }
   465	
   466	                                                break;
   467	                                        }
   468	
   469	                                        if (
   470	                                                Object.hasOwn(globals, keypath) &&
   471	                                                expression.arguments.every((arg) => arg.type !== 'SpreadElement')
   472	                                        ) {
   473	                                                const [type, fn] = globals[keypath];
   474	                                                const values = expression.arguments.map((arg) => scope.evaluate(arg));
   475	
   476	                                                if (fn && values.every((e) => e.is_known)) {
   477	                                                        this.values.add(fn(...values.map((e) => e.value)));
   478	                                                } else {
   479	                                                        this.values.add(type);
   480	                                                }
   481	
   482	                                                break;
   483	                                        }
   484	                                }
   485	
   486	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   487	                                break;
   488	                        }
   489	
   490	                        case 'TemplateLiteral': {
   491	                                let result = expression.quasis[0].value.cooked;
   492	
   493	                                for (let i = 0; i < expression.expressions.length; i += 1) {
   494	                                        const e = scope.evaluate(expression.expressions[i]);
   495	
   496	                                        if (e.is_known) {
   497	                                                result += e.value + expression.quasis[i + 1].value.cooked;
   498	                                        } else {
   499	                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   500	                                                break;
   501	                                        }
   502	                                }
   503	
   504	                                this.values.add(result);
   505	                                break;
   506	                        }
   507	
   508	                        case 'MemberExpression': {
   509	                                const keypath = get_global_keypath(expression, scope);
   510	
   511	                                if (keypath && Object.hasOwn(global_constants, keypath)) {
   512	                                        this.values.add(global_constants[keypath]);
   513	                                        break;
   514	                                }
   515	
   516	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   517	                                break;
   518	                        }
   519	
   520	                        case 'ArrowFunctionExpression':
   521	                        case 'FunctionExpression':
   522	                        case 'FunctionDeclaration': {
   523	                                this.values.add(FUNCTION);
   524	                                break;
   525	                        }
   526	
   527	                        default: {
   528	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   529	                        }
   530	                }
   531	
   532	                for (const value of this.values) {
   533	                        this.value = value; // saves having special logic for `size === 1`
   534	
   535	                        if (value !== STRING && typeof value !== 'string') {
   536	                                this.is_string = false;
   537	                        }
   538	
   539	                        if (value !== NUMBER && typeof value !== 'number') {
   540	                                this.is_number = false;
   541	                        }
   542	
   543	                        if (value !== FUNCTION) {
   544	                                this.is_function = false;
   545	                        }
   546	
   547	                        if (value == null || value === UNKNOWN) {
   548	                                this.is_defined = false;
   549	                        }
   550	
   551	                        if (value === UNKNOWN) {
   552	                                this.has_unknown = true;
   553	                        }
   554	                }
   555	
   556	                if (this.values.size > 1 || typeof this.value === 'symbol') {
   557	                        this.is_known = false;
   558	                }
   559	
   560	                current_evaluations.delete(expression);
   561	        }
   562	}
   563	
   564	export class Scope {
   565	        /** @type {ScopeRoot} */
   566	        root;
   567	
   568	        /**
   569	         * The immediate parent scope
   570	         * @type {Scope | null}
   571	         */
   572	        parent;
   573	
   574	        /**
   575	         * Whether or not `var` declarations are contained by this scope
   576	         * @type {boolean}
   577	         */
   578	        #porous;
   579	
   580	        /**
   581	         * A map of every identifier declared by this scope, and all the
   582	         * identifiers that reference it
   583	         * @type {Map<string, Binding>}
   584	         */
   585	        declarations = new Map();
   586	
   587	        /**
   588	         * A map of declarators to the bindings they declare
   589	         * @type {Map<VariableDeclarator | AST.LetDirective, Binding[]>}
   590	         */
   591	        declarators = new Map();
   592	
   593	        /**
   594	         * A set of all the names referenced with this scope
   595	         * — useful for generating unique names
   596	         * @type {Map<string, { node: Identifier; path: AST.SvelteNode[] }[]>}
   597	         */
   598	        references = new Map();
   599	
   600	        /**
   601	         * The scope depth allows us to determine if a state variable is referenced in its own scope,
   602	         * which is usually an error. Block statements do not increase this value
   603	         */
   604	        function_depth = 0;
   605	
   606	        /**
   607	         * If tracing of reactive dependencies is enabled for this scope
   608	         * @type {null | Expression}
   609	         */
   610	        tracing = null;
   611	
   612	        /**
   613	         *
   614	         * @param {ScopeRoot} root
   615	         * @param {Scope | null} parent
   616	         * @param {boolean} porous
   617	         */
   618	        constructor(root, parent, porous) {
   619	                this.root = root;
   620	                this.parent = parent;
   621	                this.#porous = porous;
   622	                this.function_depth = parent ? parent.function_depth + (porous ? 0 : 1) : 0;
   623	        }
   624	
   625	        /**
   626	         * @param {Identifier} node
   627	         * @param {Binding['kind']} kind
   628	         * @param {DeclarationKind} declaration_kind
   629	         * @param {null | Expression | FunctionDeclaration | ClassDeclaration | ImportDeclaration | AST.EachBlock | AST.SnippetBlock} initial
   630	         * @returns {Binding}
   631	         */
   632	        declare(node, kind, declaration_kind, initial = null) {
   633	                if (this.parent) {
   634	                        if (declaration_kind === 'var' && this.#porous) {
   635	                                return this.parent.declare(node, kind, declaration_kind);
   636	                        }
   637	
   638	                        if (declaration_kind === 'import') {
   639	                                return this.parent.declare(node, kind, declaration_kind, initial);
   640	                        }
   641	                }
   642	
   643	                if (this.declarations.has(node.name)) {
   644	                        const binding = this.declarations.get(node.name);
   645	                        if (binding && binding.declaration_kind !== 'var' && declaration_kind !== 'var') {
   646	                                // This also errors on function types, but that's arguably a good thing
   647	                                // declaring function twice is also caught by acorn in the parse phase
   648	                                e.declaration_duplicate(node, node.name);
   649	                        }
   650	                }
   651	
   652	                const binding = new Binding(this, node, kind, declaration_kind, initial);
   653	
   654	                validate_identifier_name(binding, this.function_depth);
   655	
   656	                this.declarations.set(node.name, binding);
   657	                this.root.conflicts.add(node.name);
   658	                return binding;
   659	        }
   660	
   661	        child(porous = false) {<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

   842	         * A map of node->associated scope. A node appearing in this map does not necessarily mean that it created a scope
   843	         * @type {Map<AST.SvelteNode, Scope>}
   844	         */
   845	        const scopes = new Map();
   846	        const scope = new Scope(root, parent, false);

   865	         * @param {Scope} scope

   869	                for (const param of params) {
   870	                        for (const node of extract_identifiers(param)) {
   871	                                scope.declare(node, 'normal', param.type === 'RestElement' ? 'rest_param' : 'param');

   874	        }

   898	        const Component = (node, context) => {

   903	                if (node.type === 'SvelteComponent') {

   905	                }

   908	                        ? context.state
   909	                        : { scope: node.metadata.scopes.default };
   910

   912	                        if (attribute.type === 'LetDirective') {
   913	                                context.visit(attribute, default_state);
   914	                        } else {

   916	                        }
   917	                }
   918

   921	
   922	                        const slot_name = determine_slot(child);
   923	
   924	                        if (slot_name !== null) {
   925	                                node.metadata.scopes[slot_name] = context.state.scope.child();
   926	
   927	                                state = {

   930	                        }
